Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1128, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 275. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 8. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 123

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test region, score 33 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 108 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 93

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 45 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 12 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 28 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 57 (Very low contrast)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 53

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 51 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 46

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 31 (Text has insufficient contrast)
  • Package tenon, test 95, score 13 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
